177 /* Return all but the first "n" matched characters back to the input stream. */
178 #define yyless(n) \
179  do \
180  { \
181  /* Undo effects of setting up yytext. */ \
182  int yyless_macro_arg = (n); \
183  YY_LESS_LINENO(yyless_macro_arg);\
184  *yy_cp = (yy_hold_char); \
185  YY_RESTORE_YY_MORE_OFFSET \
186  (yy_c_buf_p) = yy_cp = yy_bp + yyless_macro_arg - YY_MORE_ADJ; \
187  YY_DO_BEFORE_ACTION; /* set up yytext again */ \
188  } \
189  while ( 0 )

192 #ifndef YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE
193 #define YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE
194 struct yy_buffer_state
195  {
196 
197  std::streambuf* yy_input_file;
198 
199  char *yy_ch_buf; /* input buffer */
200  char *yy_buf_pos; /* current position in input buffer */
201 
202  /* Size of input buffer in bytes, not including room for EOB
203  * characters.
204  */
205  int yy_buf_size;
206 
207  /* Number of characters read into yy_ch_buf, not including EOB
208  * characters.
209  */
210  int yy_n_chars;
211 
212  /* Whether we "own" the buffer - i.e., we know we created it,
213  * and can realloc() it to grow it, and should free() it to
214  * delete it.
215  */
216  int yy_is_our_buffer;
217 
218  /* Whether this is an "interactive" input source; if so, and
219  * if we're using stdio for input, then we want to use getc()
220  * instead of fread(), to make sure we stop fetching input after
221  * each newline.
222  */
223  int yy_is_interactive;
224 
225  /* Whether we're considered to be at the beginning of a line.
226  * If so, '^' rules will be active on the next match, otherwise
227  * not.
228  */
229  int yy_at_bol;
230 
231  int yy_bs_lineno;
232  int yy_bs_column;
234  /* Whether to try to fill the input buffer when we reach the
235  * end of it.
236  */
237  int yy_fill_buffer;
238 
239  int yy_buffer_status;
240 
241 #define YY_BUFFER_NEW 0
242 #define YY_BUFFER_NORMAL 1
243  /* When an EOF's been seen but there's still some text to process
244  * then we mark the buffer as YY_EOF_PENDING, to indicate that we
245  * shouldn't try reading from the input source any more. We might
246  * still have a bunch of tokens to match, though, because of
247  * possible backing-up.
248  *
249  * When we actually see the EOF, we change the status to "new"
250  * (via yyrestart()), so that the user can continue scanning by
251  * just pointing yyin at a new input file.
252  */
253 #define YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING 2
254 
255  };
256 #endif /* !YY_STRUCT_YY_BUFFER_STATE */
257 
258 /* We provide macros for accessing buffer states in case in the
259  * future we want to put the buffer states in a more general
260  * "scanner state".
261  *
262  * Returns the top of the stack, or NULL.

264 #define YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ( (yy_buffer_stack) \
265  ? (yy_buffer_stack)[(yy_buffer_stack_top)] \
266  : NULL)
267 /* Same as previous macro, but useful when we know that the buffer stack is not
268  * NULL or when we need an lvalue. For internal use only.
269  */
270 #define YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE (yy_buffer_stack)[(yy_buffer_stack_top)]

5905  yy_current_state = yy_get_previous_state( );
5906 
5907  yy_cp = (yy_c_buf_p);
5908  yy_bp = (yytext_ptr) + YY_MORE_ADJ;
5909  goto yy_find_action;
5910  }
5911  break;
5912  }
5913 
5914  default:
5915  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
5916  "fatal flex scanner internal error--no action found" );
5917  } /* end of action switch */
5918  } /* end of scanning one token */
5919  } /* end of user's declarations */
5920 } /* end of yylex */

6007 #ifdef YY_INTERACTIVE
6008 int yyFlexLexer::LexerInput( char* buf, int /* max_size */ )

6011 #endif

6014  return 0;

6018

6020  return 0;
6021 
6022  if ( yyin.bad() )
6023  return -1;
6024 
6025  return 1;
6026 
6027 #else

6029

6031  return -1;

6042 /* yy_get_next_buffer - try to read in a new buffer
6043  *
6044  * Returns a code representing an action:
6045  * EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH -
6046  * EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN - continue scanning from current position
6047  * EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE - end of file
6048  */
6049 int yyFlexLexer::yy_get_next_buffer()
6050 {
6051  char *dest = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf;
6052  char *source = (yytext_ptr);
6053  int number_to_move, i;
6054  int ret_val;
6055 
6056  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) > &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars) + 1] )
6057  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
6058  "fatal flex scanner internal error--end of buffer missed" );
6059 
6060  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_fill_buffer == 0 )
6061  { /* Don't try to fill the buffer, so this is an EOF. */
6062  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr) - YY_MORE_ADJ == 1 )
6063  {
6064  /* We matched a single character, the EOB, so
6065  * treat this as a final EOF.
6066  */
6067  return EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
6068  }
6069 
6070  else
6071  {
6072  /* We matched some text prior to the EOB, first
6073  * process it.
6074  */
6075  return EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
6076  }
6077  }
6078 
6079  /* Try to read more data. */
6080 
6081  /* First move last chars to start of buffer. */
6082  number_to_move = (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr) - 1);
6083 
6084  for ( i = 0; i < number_to_move; ++i )
6085  *(dest++) = *(source++);
6086 
6087  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status == YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING )
6088  /* don't do the read, it's not guaranteed to return an EOF,
6089  * just force an EOF
6090  */
6091  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars) = 0;
6092 
6093  else
6094  {
6095  int num_to_read =
6096  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size - number_to_move - 1;
6097 
6098  while ( num_to_read <= 0 )
6099  { /* Not enough room in the buffer - grow it. */
6100 
6101  /* just a shorter name for the current buffer */
6102  YY_BUFFER_STATE b = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE;
6103 
6104  int yy_c_buf_p_offset =
6105  (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - b->yy_ch_buf);
6106 
6107  if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
6108  {
6109  int new_size = b->yy_buf_size * 2;
6110 
6111  if ( new_size <= 0 )
6112  b->yy_buf_size += b->yy_buf_size / 8;
6113  else
6114  b->yy_buf_size *= 2;
6115 
6116  b->yy_ch_buf = (char *)
6117  /* Include room in for 2 EOB chars. */
6118  yyrealloc( (void *) b->yy_ch_buf,
6119  (yy_size_t) (b->yy_buf_size + 2) );
6120  }
6121  else
6122  /* Can't grow it, we don't own it. */
6123  b->yy_ch_buf = NULL;
6124 
6125  if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
6126  YY_FATAL_ERROR(
6127  "fatal error - scanner input buffer overflow" );
6128 
6129  (yy_c_buf_p) = &b->yy_ch_buf[yy_c_buf_p_offset];
6130 
6131  num_to_read = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size -
6132  number_to_move - 1;
6133 
6134  }
6135 
6136  if ( num_to_read > YY_READ_BUF_SIZE )
6137  num_to_read = YY_READ_BUF_SIZE;
6138 
6139  /* Read in more data. */
6140  YY_INPUT( (&YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move]),
6141  (yy_n_chars), num_to_read );
6142 
6143  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
6144  }
6145 
6146  if ( (yy_n_chars) == 0 )
6147  {
6148  if ( number_to_move == YY_MORE_ADJ )
6149  {
6150  ret_val = EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE;
6151  yyrestart( yyin );
6152  }
6153 
6154  else
6155  {
6156  ret_val = EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH;
6157  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buffer_status =
6158  YY_BUFFER_EOF_PENDING;
6159  }
6160  }
6161 
6162  else
6163  ret_val = EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN;
6164 
6165  if (((yy_n_chars) + number_to_move) > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size) {
6166  /* Extend the array by 50%, plus the number we really need. */
6167  int new_size = (yy_n_chars) + number_to_move + ((yy_n_chars) >> 1);
6168  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf = (char *) yyrealloc(
6169  (void *) YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf, (yy_size_t) new_size );
6170  if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
6171  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_get_next_buffer()" );
6172  /* "- 2" to take care of EOB's */
6173  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size = (int) (new_size - 2);
6174  }
6175 
6176  (yy_n_chars) += number_to_move;
6177  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars)] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
6178  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars) + 1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
6179 
6180  (yytext_ptr) = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[0];
6181 
6182  return ret_val;
6183 }
6184 
6185 /* yy_get_previous_state - get the state just before the EOB char was reached */
6186 
6187  yy_state_type yyFlexLexer::yy_get_previous_state()
6188 {
6189  yy_state_type yy_current_state;
6190  char *yy_cp;
6191 
6192  yy_current_state = (yy_start);
6193 
6194  for ( yy_cp = (yytext_ptr) + YY_MORE_ADJ; yy_cp < (yy_c_buf_p); ++yy_cp )
6195  {
6196  if ( *yy_cp )
6197  {
6198  yy_current_state = yy_nxt[yy_current_state][YY_SC_TO_UI(*yy_cp)];
6199  }
6200  else
6201  yy_current_state = yy_NUL_trans[yy_current_state];
6202  if ( yy_accept[yy_current_state] )
6203  {
6204  (yy_last_accepting_state) = yy_current_state;
6205  (yy_last_accepting_cpos) = yy_cp;
6206  }
6207  }
6208 
6209  return yy_current_state;
6210 }
6211 
6212 /* yy_try_NUL_trans - try to make a transition on the NUL character
6213  *
6214  * synopsis
6215  * next_state = yy_try_NUL_trans( current_state );
6216  */
6217  yy_state_type yyFlexLexer::yy_try_NUL_trans( yy_state_type yy_current_state )
6218 {
6219  int yy_is_jam;
6220  char *yy_cp = (yy_c_buf_p);
6221 
6222  yy_current_state = yy_NUL_trans[yy_current_state];
6223  yy_is_jam = (yy_current_state == 0);
6224 
6225  if ( ! yy_is_jam )
6226  {
6227  if ( yy_accept[yy_current_state] )
6228  {
6229  (yy_last_accepting_state) = yy_current_state;
6230  (yy_last_accepting_cpos) = yy_cp;
6231  }
6232  }
6233 
6234  return yy_is_jam ? 0 : yy_current_state;
6235 }
6236 
6237 #ifndef YY_NO_UNPUT
6238  void yyFlexLexer::yyunput( int c, char* yy_bp)
6239 {
6240  char *yy_cp;
6241 
6242  yy_cp = (yy_c_buf_p);
6243 
6244  /* undo effects of setting up yytext */
6245  *yy_cp = (yy_hold_char);
6246 
6247  if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
6248  { /* need to shift things up to make room */
6249  /* +2 for EOB chars. */
6250  int number_to_move = (yy_n_chars) + 2;
6251  char *dest = &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[
6252  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size + 2];
6253  char *source =
6254  &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[number_to_move];
6255 
6256  while ( source > YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf )
6257  *--dest = *--source;
6258 
6259  yy_cp += (int) (dest - source);
6260  yy_bp += (int) (dest - source);
6261  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars =
6262  (yy_n_chars) = (int) YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_size;
6263 
6264  if ( yy_cp < YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf + 2 )
6265  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "flex scanner push-back overflow" );
6266  }
6267 
6268  *--yy_cp = (char) c;
6269 
6270  (yytext_ptr) = yy_bp;
6271  (yy_hold_char) = *yy_cp;
6272  (yy_c_buf_p) = yy_cp;
6273 }
6274 #endif
6275 
6276  int yyFlexLexer::yyinput()
6277 {
6278  int c;
6279 
6280  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
6281 
6282  if ( *(yy_c_buf_p) == YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR )
6283  {
6284  /* yy_c_buf_p now points to the character we want to return.
6285  * If this occurs *before* the EOB characters, then it's a
6286  * valid NUL; if not, then we've hit the end of the buffer.
6287  */
6288  if ( (yy_c_buf_p) < &YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_ch_buf[(yy_n_chars)] )
6289  /* This was really a NUL. */
6290  *(yy_c_buf_p) = '\0';
6291 
6292  else
6293  { /* need more input */
6294  int offset = (int) ((yy_c_buf_p) - (yytext_ptr));
6295  ++(yy_c_buf_p);
6296 
6297  switch ( yy_get_next_buffer( ) )
6298  {
6299  case EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH:
6300  /* This happens because yy_g_n_b()
6301  * sees that we've accumulated a
6302  * token and flags that we need to
6303  * try matching the token before
6304  * proceeding. But for input(),
6305  * there's no matching to consider.
6306  * So convert the EOB_ACT_LAST_MATCH
6307  * to EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE.
6308  */
6309 
6310  /* Reset buffer status. */
6311  yyrestart( yyin );
6312 
6313  /*FALLTHROUGH*/
6314 
6315  case EOB_ACT_END_OF_FILE:
6316  {
6317  if ( yywrap( ) )
6318  return 0;
6319 
6320  if ( ! (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) )
6321  YY_NEW_FILE;
6322 #ifdef __cplusplus
6323  return yyinput();
6324 #else
6325  return input();
6326 #endif
6327  }
6328 
6329  case EOB_ACT_CONTINUE_SCAN:
6330  (yy_c_buf_p) = (yytext_ptr) + offset;
6331  break;
6332  }
6333  }
6334  }
6335 
6336  c = *(unsigned char *) (yy_c_buf_p); /* cast for 8-bit char's */
6337  *(yy_c_buf_p) = '\0'; /* preserve yytext */
6338  (yy_hold_char) = *++(yy_c_buf_p);
6339 
6340  return c;
6341 }
6342 
6348  void yyFlexLexer::yyrestart( std::istream& input_file )
6349 {
6350 
6351  if ( ! YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ){
6352  yyensure_buffer_stack ();
6353  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE =
6354  yy_create_buffer( yyin, YY_BUF_SIZE );
6355  }
6356 
6357  yy_init_buffer( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER, input_file );
6358  yy_load_buffer_state( );
6359 }
6360 
6366 void yyFlexLexer::yyrestart( std::istream* input_file )
6367 {
6368  if( ! input_file ) {
6369  input_file = &yyin;
6370  }
6371  yyrestart( *input_file );
6372 }
6373 
6378  void yyFlexLexer::yy_switch_to_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE new_buffer )
6379 {
6380 
6381  /* TODO. We should be able to replace this entire function body
6382  * with
6383  * yypop_buffer_state();
6384  * yypush_buffer_state(new_buffer);
6385  */
6386  yyensure_buffer_stack ();
6387  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER == new_buffer )
6388  return;
6389 
6390  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
6391  {
6392  /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
6393  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
6394  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = (yy_c_buf_p);
6395  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
6396  }
6397 
6398  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
6399  yy_load_buffer_state( );
6400 
6401  /* We don't actually know whether we did this switch during
6402  * EOF (yywrap()) processing, but the only time this flag
6403  * is looked at is after yywrap() is called, so it's safe
6404  * to go ahead and always set it.
6405  */
6406  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
6407 }
6408 
6409  void yyFlexLexer::yy_load_buffer_state()
6410 {
6411  (yy_n_chars) = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars;
6412  (yytext_ptr) = (yy_c_buf_p) = YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos;
6413  yyin.rdbuf(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_input_file);
6414  (yy_hold_char) = *(yy_c_buf_p);
6415 }
6416 
6423  YY_BUFFER_STATE yyFlexLexer::yy_create_buffer( std::istream& file, int size )
6424 {
6425  YY_BUFFER_STATE b;
6426 
6427  b = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) yyalloc( sizeof( struct yy_buffer_state ) );
6428  if ( ! b )
6429  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_create_buffer()" );
6430 
6431  b->yy_buf_size = size;
6432 
6433  /* yy_ch_buf has to be 2 characters longer than the size given because
6434  * we need to put in 2 end-of-buffer characters.
6435  */
6436  b->yy_ch_buf = (char *) yyalloc( (yy_size_t) (b->yy_buf_size + 2) );
6437  if ( ! b->yy_ch_buf )
6438  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yy_create_buffer()" );
6439 
6440  b->yy_is_our_buffer = 1;
6441 
6442  yy_init_buffer( b, file );
6443 
6444  return b;
6445 }
6446 
6453  YY_BUFFER_STATE yyFlexLexer::yy_create_buffer( std::istream* file, int size )
6454 {
6455  return yy_create_buffer( *file, size );
6456 }
6457 
6462  void yyFlexLexer::yy_delete_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b )
6463 {
6464 
6465  if ( ! b )
6466  return;
6467 
6468  if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER ) /* Not sure if we should pop here. */
6469  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = (YY_BUFFER_STATE) 0;
6470 
6471  if ( b->yy_is_our_buffer )
6472  yyfree( (void *) b->yy_ch_buf );
6473 
6474  yyfree( (void *) b );
6475 }
6476 
6477 /* Initializes or reinitializes a buffer.
6478  * This function is sometimes called more than once on the same buffer,
6479  * such as during a yyrestart() or at EOF.
6480  */
6481  void yyFlexLexer::yy_init_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b, std::istream& file )
6482 
6483 {
6484  int oerrno = errno;
6485 
6486  yy_flush_buffer( b );
6487 
6488  b->yy_input_file = file.rdbuf();
6489  b->yy_fill_buffer = 1;
6490 
6491  /* If b is the current buffer, then yy_init_buffer was _probably_
6492  * called from yyrestart() or through yy_get_next_buffer.
6493  * In that case, we don't want to reset the lineno or column.
6494  */
6495  if (b != YY_CURRENT_BUFFER){
6496  b->yy_bs_lineno = 1;
6497  b->yy_bs_column = 0;
6498  }
6499 
6500  b->yy_is_interactive = 0;
6501  errno = oerrno;
6502 }
6503 
6508  void yyFlexLexer::yy_flush_buffer( YY_BUFFER_STATE b )
6509 {
6510  if ( ! b )
6511  return;
6512 
6513  b->yy_n_chars = 0;
6514 
6515  /* We always need two end-of-buffer characters. The first causes
6516  * a transition to the end-of-buffer state. The second causes
6517  * a jam in that state.
6518  */
6519  b->yy_ch_buf[0] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
6520  b->yy_ch_buf[1] = YY_END_OF_BUFFER_CHAR;
6521 
6522  b->yy_buf_pos = &b->yy_ch_buf[0];
6523 
6524  b->yy_at_bol = 1;
6525  b->yy_buffer_status = YY_BUFFER_NEW;
6526 
6527  if ( b == YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
6528  yy_load_buffer_state( );
6529 }
6530 
6537 void yyFlexLexer::yypush_buffer_state (YY_BUFFER_STATE new_buffer)
6538 {
6539  if (new_buffer == NULL)
6540  return;
6541 
6542  yyensure_buffer_stack();
6543 
6544  /* This block is copied from yy_switch_to_buffer. */
6545  if ( YY_CURRENT_BUFFER )
6546  {
6547  /* Flush out information for old buffer. */
6548  *(yy_c_buf_p) = (yy_hold_char);
6549  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_buf_pos = (yy_c_buf_p);
6550  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE->yy_n_chars = (yy_n_chars);
6551  }
6552 
6553  /* Only push if top exists. Otherwise, replace top. */
6554  if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
6555  (yy_buffer_stack_top)++;
6556  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = new_buffer;
6557 
6558  /* copied from yy_switch_to_buffer. */
6559  yy_load_buffer_state( );
6560  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
6561 }
6562 
6567 void yyFlexLexer::yypop_buffer_state (void)
6568 {
6569  if (!YY_CURRENT_BUFFER)
6570  return;
6571 
6572  yy_delete_buffer(YY_CURRENT_BUFFER );
6573  YY_CURRENT_BUFFER_LVALUE = NULL;
6574  if ((yy_buffer_stack_top) > 0)
6575  --(yy_buffer_stack_top);
6576 
6577  if (YY_CURRENT_BUFFER) {
6578  yy_load_buffer_state( );
6579  (yy_did_buffer_switch_on_eof) = 1;
6580  }
6581 }
6582 
6583 /* Allocates the stack if it does not exist.
6584  * Guarantees space for at least one push.
6585  */
6586 void yyFlexLexer::yyensure_buffer_stack(void)
6587 {
6588  yy_size_t num_to_alloc;
6589 
6590  if (!(yy_buffer_stack)) {
6591 
6592  /* First allocation is just for 2 elements, since we don't know if this
6593  * scanner will even need a stack. We use 2 instead of 1 to avoid an
6594  * immediate realloc on the next call.
6595  */
6596  num_to_alloc = 1; /* After all that talk, this was set to 1 anyways... */
6597  (yy_buffer_stack) = (struct yy_buffer_state**)yyalloc
6598  (num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
6599  );
6600  if ( ! (yy_buffer_stack) )
6601  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yyensure_buffer_stack()" );
6602 
6603  memset((yy_buffer_stack), 0, num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
6604 
6605  (yy_buffer_stack_max) = num_to_alloc;
6606  (yy_buffer_stack_top) = 0;
6607  return;
6608  }
6609 
6610  if ((yy_buffer_stack_top) >= ((yy_buffer_stack_max)) - 1){
6611 
6612  /* Increase the buffer to prepare for a possible push. */
6613  yy_size_t grow_size = 8 /* arbitrary grow size */;
6614 
6615  num_to_alloc = (yy_buffer_stack_max) + grow_size;
6616  (yy_buffer_stack) = (struct yy_buffer_state**)yyrealloc
6617  ((yy_buffer_stack),
6618  num_to_alloc * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*)
6619  );
6620  if ( ! (yy_buffer_stack) )
6621  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of dynamic memory in yyensure_buffer_stack()" );
6622 
6623  /* zero only the new slots.*/
6624  memset((yy_buffer_stack) + (yy_buffer_stack_max), 0, grow_size * sizeof(struct yy_buffer_state*));
6625  (yy_buffer_stack_max) = num_to_alloc;
6626  }
6627 }
6628 
6629  void yyFlexLexer::yy_push_state( int _new_state )
6630 {
6631  if ( (yy_start_stack_ptr) >= (yy_start_stack_depth) )
6632  {
6633  yy_size_t new_size;
6634 
6635  (yy_start_stack_depth) += YY_START_STACK_INCR;
6636  new_size = (yy_size_t) (yy_start_stack_depth) * sizeof( int );
6637 
6638  if ( ! (yy_start_stack) )
6639  (yy_start_stack) = (int *) yyalloc( new_size );
6640 
6641  else
6642  (yy_start_stack) = (int *) yyrealloc(
6643  (void *) (yy_start_stack), new_size );
6644 
6645  if ( ! (yy_start_stack) )
6646  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "out of memory expanding start-condition stack" );
6647  }
6648 
6649  (yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr)++] = YY_START;
6650 
6651  BEGIN(_new_state);
6652 }
6653 
6654  void yyFlexLexer::yy_pop_state()
6655 {
6656  if ( --(yy_start_stack_ptr) < 0 )
6657  YY_FATAL_ERROR( "start-condition stack underflow" );
6658 
6659  BEGIN((yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr)]);
6660 }
6661 
6662  int yyFlexLexer::yy_top_state()
6663 {
6664  return (yy_start_stack)[(yy_start_stack_ptr) - 1];
6665 }

6726 void *yyrealloc (void * ptr, yy_size_t size )
6727 {
6728 
6729  /* The cast to (char *) in the following accommodates both
6730  * implementations that use char* generic pointers, and those
6731  * that use void* generic pointers. It works with the latter
6732  * because both ANSI C and C++ allow castless assignment from
6733  * any pointer type to void*, and deal with argument conversions
6734  * as though doing an assignment.
6735  */
6736  return realloc(ptr, size);
